Signup.c(34):     /***************************************************************\n
Signup.c(34):     ** define and instantiate validation objects\n
Signup.c(34):     ** the validation object accepts the following parameters:\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   realName: name used in the alerts (same as label on the page)\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   formEltName: this must be the name of the corresponding\n
Signup.c(34):     **       HTML form element; make it the same as the object name\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   eltType: element type (we have to create this since IE3\n
Signup.c(34):     **       doesn't support the type property for for elements)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     text\n
Signup.c(34):     **     textarea\n
Signup.c(34):     **     checkbox\n
Signup.c(34):     **     radio\n
Signup.c(34):     **     select\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   uptoSnuff: function call that's evaluated during validation check\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isText(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isSelect(formObj)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isRadio(formObj)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isCheck(formObj, form, [index of first checkbox in group],\n
Signup.c(34):     **         [number of checkboxes])\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isEmail(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isState(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isZipCode(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isPhoneNum(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isDate(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   format: text representation of required format;\n
Signup.c(34):     **       pass 'null' if no required format;\n
Signup.c(34):     **       used in alert as an aid to user\n
Signup.c(34):     ***************************************************************/\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     // object definition\n
Signup.c(34):     function validation(realName, formEltName, eltType, upToSnuff, format) {\n
Signup.c(34):       this.realName = realName;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.formEltName = formEltName;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.eltType = eltType;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.upToSnuff = upToSnuff;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.format = format;\n
Signup.c(34):     }\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     /***************************************************************\n
Signup.c(34):     ** create a new object for each form element you need to validate\n
Signup.c(34):     ** for example:\n
Signup.c(34):     ** var lastName = new validation('last name', 'lastName', 'text', 'isText(str)', null);\n
Signup.c(34):     ** var phoneNum = new validation('phone number', 'phoneNum', 'text', 'isPhoneNum(str)', 'x
Signup.c(34):     xx-xxx-xxxx');\n
Signup.c(34):     ** var reason = new validation('reason for reading this', 'reason', 'checkbox', 'isCheck(f
Signup.c(34):     ormObj, form, 14, 3)', null);\n
Signup.c(34):     ***************************************************************/\n
Signup.c(34):     // create objects here:\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     var username = new validation('a username', 'username', 'text', 'isText(str)', null);\n
Signup.c(34):     var password = new validation('a password', 'password', 'text', 'isText(str)', null);\n
Signup.c(34):     var passwordC = new validation('a password confirmation', 'passwordConfirm', 'text', 'isTe

Signup.c(34):     var address = new validation('your address', 'address1', 'text', 'isText(str)', null);\n
Signup.c(34):     var csz = new validation('your City/State/Zip', 'address2', 'text', 'isText(str)', null);\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     /***************************************************************\n
Signup.c(34):     ** Define the elts array:\n
Signup.c(34):     ** Add a new item to the array for each object you create above\n
Signup.c(34):     ** Make sure the value of the array element is the same as\n
Signup.c(34):     ** the name of the object, and that the array elements are listed\n
Signup.c(34):     ** in the same order the corresponding objects appear in the form\n
Signup.c(34):     ** (it's more clear to the user that way)\n
Signup.c(34):     ** for example:\n
Signup.c(34):     ** var elts = new Array(lastName, phoneNum, reason)\n

Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     /***************************************************************\n
Signup.c(34):     ** The main function keeps track of which fields the user missed\n
Signup.c(34):     ** or filled in incorrectly, and alerts the user so they can go\n
Signup.c(34):     ** back and fix what's wrong.\n

Signup.c(34):     ** validate existence of input\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isText(str): verifies text input or textarea is not empty\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isSelect(formObj): verifies item from a select menu is chosen\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isRadio(formObj): verifies one of a group of radio buttons is chosen\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isCheck(formObj, form, [begin], [num]): verifies at least one\n
Signup.c(34):     **       of a group of checkboxes is checked\n
Signup.c(34):     **     for [begin], fill in the index number in the elements array\n
Signup.c(34):     **         of the first checkbox (remember to start counting from zero)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     for [num], fill in the number of checkboxes in the group\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     ** validate text in text input or textarea matches pattern\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isEmail(str): verifies email address (contains "@" and ".")\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isState(str): verifies U.S. State Code\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isZipCode(str): verifies zip code of form xxxxx or xxxxx-xxxx\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isPhoneNum(str): verifies phone number of form xxx-xxx-xxxx\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isDate(str): verifies date of form mm/dd/yyyy\n
Signup.c(34):     ***************************************************************/\n

Signup.c(34):       return (str != "");\n

Signup.c(34):       return (formObj.selectedIndex != 0);\n
Signup.c(34):     }\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     function isRadio(formObj) {\n
Signup.c(34):       for (j=0; j<formObj.length; j++) {\n
Signup.c(34):         if (formObj[j].checked) {\n
Signup.c(34):           return true;\n
Signup.c(34):         }\n
Signup.c(34):       }\n
Signup.c(34):       return false;\n
Signup.c(34):     }\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     function isCheck(formObj, form, begin, num) {\n
Signup.c(34):       for (j=begin; j<begin+num; j++) {\n
Signup.c(34):         if (form.elements[j].checked) {\n
Signup.c(34):           return true;\n
Signup.c(34):         }\n
Signup.c(34):       }\n
Signup.c(34):       return false;\n
Signup.c(34):     }\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     function isEmail(str) {\n
Signup.c(34):       return ((str != "") && (str.indexOf("@") != -1) && (str.indexOf(".") != -1));\n
Signup.c(34):     }\n
Signup.c(34):     \n

Signup.c(34):     ** define and instantiate validation objects\n
Signup.c(34):     ** the validation object accepts the following parameters:\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   realName: name used in the alerts (same as label on the page)\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   formEltName: this must be the name of the corresponding\n
Signup.c(34):     **       HTML form element; make it the same as the object name\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   eltType: element type (we have to create this since IE3\n
Signup.c(34):     **       doesn't support the type property for for elements)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     text\n
Signup.c(34):     **     textarea\n
Signup.c(34):     **     checkbox\n
Signup.c(34):     **     radio\n
Signup.c(34):     **     select\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   uptoSnuff: function call that's evaluated during validation check\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isText(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isSelect(formObj)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isRadio(formObj)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isCheck(formObj, form, [index of first checkbox in group],\n
Signup.c(34):     **         [number of checkboxes])\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isEmail(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isState(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isZipCode(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isPhoneNum(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isDate(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   format: text representation of required format;\n
Signup.c(34):     **       pass 'null' if no required format;\n
Signup.c(34):     **       used in alert as an aid to user\n
Signup.c(34):     ***************************************************************/\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     // object definition\n

Signup.c(34):       this.formEltName = formEltName;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.eltType = eltType;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.upToSnuff = upToSnuff;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.format = format;\n
Signup.c(34):     }\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     /***************************************************************\n
Signup.c(34):     ** create a new object for each form element you need to validate\n

Signup.c(34):     ** var phoneNum = new validation('phone number', 'phoneNum', 'text', 'isPhoneNum(str)', 'x
Signup.c(34):     xx-xxx-xxxx');\n

Signup.c(34):     // create objects here:\n

Signup.c(34):     \n

Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   realName: name used in the alerts (same as label on the page)\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   formEltName: this must be the name of the corresponding\n

Signup.c(34):     **   eltType: element type (we have to create this since IE3\n
Signup.c(34):     **       doesn't support the type property for for elements)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     text\n

Signup.c(34):     **     radio\n
Signup.c(34):     **     select\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   uptoSnuff: function call that's evaluated during validation check\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isText(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isSelect(formObj)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isRadio(formObj)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isCheck(formObj, form, [index of first checkbox in group],\n
Signup.c(34):     **         [number of checkboxes])\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isEmail(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isState(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isZipCode(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isPhoneNum(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     isDate(str)\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     **   format: text representation of required format;\n
Signup.c(34):     **       pass 'null' if no required format;\n
Signup.c(34):     **       used in alert as an aid to user\n
Signup.c(34):     ***************************************************************/\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     // object definition\n
Signup.c(34):     function validation(realName, formEltName, eltType, upToSnuff, format) {\n
Signup.c(34):       this.realName = realName;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.formEltName = formEltName;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.eltType = eltType;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.upToSnuff = upToSnuff;\n
Signup.c(34):       this.format = format;\n
Signup.c(34):     }\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     /***************************************************************\n
Signup.c(34):     ** create a new object for each form element you need to validate\n
Signup.c(34):     ** for example:\n
Signup.c(34):     ** var lastName = new validation('last name', 'lastName', 'text', 'isText(str)', null);\n
Signup.c(34):     ** var phoneNum = new validation('phone number', 'phoneNum', 'text', 'isPhoneNum(str)', 'x
Signup.c(34):     xx-xxx-xxxx');\n

Signup.c(34):     // create objects here:\n
Signup.c(34):     \n

Signup.c(34):     var username = new validation('a username', 'username', 'text', 'isText(str)', null);\n

Signup.c(34):     /***************************************************************\n
Signup.c(34):     ** The main function keeps track of which fields the user missed\n
Signup.c(34):     ** or filled in incorrectly, and alerts the user so they can go\n
Signup.c(34):     ** back and fix what's wrong.\n
Signup.c(34):     ** Set allAtOnce to true if you want this "validation help" to\n
Signup.c(34):     ** alert the user to all mistakes at once; set it to false if\n
Signup.c(34):     ** you want it to show one mistake at a time\n
Signup.c(34):     ***************************************************************/\n

Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     /***************************************************************\n
Signup.c(34):     ** change text for alerts here\n
Signup.c(34):     ** unspecified field (text): "Please include [field name]."\n
Signup.c(34):     ** unspecified field (other): "Please choose [field name]."\n
Signup.c(34):     ** invalid text field entries: "[field value] is an invalid [field name]!"\n
Signup.c(34):     ** help with format: "Use this format: "\n
Signup.c(34):     ***************************************************************/\n
Signup.c(34):     var beginRequestAlertForText = "Please include ";\n
Signup.c(34):     var beginRequestAlertGeneric = "Please choose ";\n
Signup.c(34):     var endRequestAlert = ".";\n
Signup.c(34):     var beginInvalidAlert = " is an invalid ";\n
Signup.c(34):     var endInvalidAlert = "!";\n
Signup.c(34):     var beginFormatAlert = "  Use this format: ";\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     /***************************************************************\n
Signup.c(34):     ** these functions validate the string or form object passed in,\n
Signup.c(34):     ** and return true or false based on whether the test succeeds or fails\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     ** validate existence of input\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isText(str): verifies text input or textarea is not empty\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isSelect(formObj): verifies item from a select menu is chosen\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isRadio(formObj): verifies one of a group of radio buttons is chosen\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isCheck(formObj, form, [begin], [num]): verifies at least one\n
Signup.c(34):     **       of a group of checkboxes is checked\n
Signup.c(34):     **     for [begin], fill in the index number in the elements array\n
Signup.c(34):     **         of the first checkbox (remember to start counting from zero)\n
Signup.c(34):     **     for [num], fill in the number of checkboxes in the group\n
Signup.c(34):     **\n
Signup.c(34):     ** validate text in text input or textarea matches pattern\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isEmail(str): verifies email address (contains "@" and ".")\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isState(str): verifies U.S. State Code\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isZipCode(str): verifies zip code of form xxxxx or xxxxx-xxxx\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isPhoneNum(str): verifies phone number of form xxx-xxx-xxxx\n
Signup.c(34):     **   isDate(str): verifies date of form mm/dd/yyyy\n
Signup.c(34):     ***************************************************************/\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     function isText(str) {\n
Signup.c(34):       return (str != "");\n
Signup.c(34):     }\n
Signup.c(34):     \n
Signup.c(34):     function isSelect(formObj) {\n
Signup.c(34):       return (formObj.selectedIndex != 0);\n
Signup.c(34):     }\n
